422static gboolean changed_cb_called;
423
424static void
425changed_cb (GSettings *settings,
426 const gchar *key,
427 gpointer data)
428{
429 changed_cb_called = TRUE(!(0));
430
431 g_assert_cmpstr (key, ==, data)do { const char *__s1 = (key), *__s2 = (data); if (g_strcmp0 (
__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 431, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "key" " " "==" " " "data", __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0);
432}
433
434/* Test that basic change notification with the changed signal works.
435 */
436static void
437test_changes (void)
438{
439 GSettings *settings;
440 GSettings *settings2;
441
442 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
443
444 g_signal_connect (settings, "changed",g_signal_connect_data ((settings), ("changed"), (((GCallback)
(changed_cb))), ("greeting"), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags) 0)
445 G_CALLBACK (changed_cb), "greeting")g_signal_connect_data ((settings), ("changed"), (((GCallback)
(changed_cb))), ("greeting"), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags) 0);
446
447 changed_cb_called = FALSE(0);
448
449 g_settings_set (settings, "greeting", "s", "new greeting");
450 g_assert_true (changed_cb_called)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (changed_cb_called) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_
= 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 450, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "'" "changed_cb_called" "' should be TRUE"); } while (0);
451
452 settings2 = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
453
454 changed_cb_called = FALSE(0);
455
456 g_settings_set (settings2, "greeting", "s", "hi");
457 g_assert_true (changed_cb_called)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_

583/* Test that reverting unapplied changes in a delay-apply
584 * settings instance works.
585 */
586static void
587test_delay_revert (void)
588{
589 GSettings *settings;
590 GSettings *settings2;
591 gchar *str;
592
593 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
594 settings2 = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
595
596 g_settings_set (settings2, "greeting", "s", "top o' the morning");
597
598 g_settings_get (settings, "greeting", "s", &str);
599 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "top o' the morning")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("top o' the morning")
; if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 599, ((const char*)
(__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"top o' the morning\"", __s1
, "==", __s2); } while (0);
600 g_free (str);
601
602 g_settings_delay (settings);
603
604 g_settings_set (settings, "greeting", "s", "greetings from test_delay_revert");
605
606 g_settings_get (settings, "greeting", "s", &str);
607 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "greetings from test_delay_revert")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("greetings from test_delay_revert"
); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 607, ((const char*)
(__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"greetings from test_delay_revert\""
, __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0);
608 g_free (str);
609 str = NULL((void*)0);
610
611 g_settings_get (settings2, "greeting", "s", &str);
612 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "top o' the morning")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("top o' the morning")
; if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 612, ((const char*)
(__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"top o' the morning\"", __s1
, "==", __s2); } while (0);
613 g_free (str);
614 str = NULL((void*)0);
615
616 g_assert_true (g_settings_get_has_unapplied (settings))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (g_settings_get_has_unapplied (settings)) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
616, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_get_has_unapplied (settings)"
"' should be TRUE"); } while (0);

619
620 g_assert_false (g_settings_get_has_unapplied (settings))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_get_has_unapplied (settings))) _g_boolean_var_

g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
620, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_get_has_unapplied (settings)"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
621

623 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "top o' the morning")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("top o' the morning")
; if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 623, ((const char*)
(__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"top o' the morning\"", __s1

636static void
637test_delay_child (void)
638{
639 GSettings *base;
640 GSettings *settings;
641 GSettings *child;
642 guint8 byte;
643 gboolean delay;
644
645 base = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.basic-types");
646 g_settings_set (base, "test-byte", "y", 36);
647
648 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
649 g_settings_delay (settings);
650 g_object_get (settings, "delay-apply", &delay, NULL((void*)0));
651 g_assert_true (delay)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (delay) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_
; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 651, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "delay" "' should be TRUE"
); } while (0);
652
653 child = g_settings_get_child (settings, "basic-types");
654 g_assert_nonnull (child)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if ((child) != ((void*)0)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_
= 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 654, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "'" "child" "' should not be NULL"); } while (0);
655
656 g_object_get (child, "delay-apply", &delay, NULL((void*)0));
657 g_assert_false (delay)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(delay)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0
; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 657, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "'" "delay" "' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
658
659 g_settings_get (child, "test-byte", "y", &byte);
660 g_assert_cmpuint (byte, ==, 36)do { guint64 __n1 = (byte), __n2 = (36); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 660, ((const char*) (__func__)), "byte" " " "==" " " "36", (
long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0
);
661
662 g_settings_set (child, "test-byte", "y", 42);
663
664 /* make sure the child was delayed too */
665 g_settings_get (base, "test-byte", "y", &byte);
666 g_assert_cmpuint (byte, ==, 36)do { guint64 __n1 = (byte), __n2 = (36); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 666, ((const char*) (__func__)), "byte" " " "==" " " "36", (
long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0
);
667
668 g_object_unref (child);
669 g_object_unref (settings);
670 g_object_unref (base);
671}

698/* Check that delay-applied changes appear atomically.
699 * More specifically, verify that all changed keys appear
700 * with their new value while handling the change-event signal.
701 */
702static void
703test_atomic (void)
704{
705 GSettings *settings;
706 GSettings *settings2;
707 gchar *str;
708
709 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
710 settings2 = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
711
712 g_settings_set (settings2, "greeting", "s", "top o' the morning");
713
714 changed_cb_called = FALSE(0);
715 changed_cb_called2 = FALSE(0);
716
717 g_signal_connect (settings2, "change-event",g_signal_connect_data ((settings2), ("change-event"), (((GCallback
) (keys_changed_cb))), (((void*)0)), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags
) 0)
718 G_CALLBACK (keys_changed_cb), NULL)g_signal_connect_data ((settings2), ("change-event"), (((GCallback
) (keys_changed_cb))), (((void*)0)), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags
) 0);
719
720 g_settings_delay (settings);
721
722 g_settings_set (settings, "greeting", "s", "greetings from test_atomic");
723 g_settings_set (settings, "farewell", "s", "atomic bye-bye");
724
725 g_settings_apply (settings);
726
727 g_settings_get (settings, "greeting", "s", &str);
728 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "greetings from test_atomic")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("greetings from test_atomic"
); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 728, ((const char*)
(__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"greetings from test_atomic\""
, __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0);
729 g_free (str);
730 str = NULL((void*)0);
731
732 g_settings_get (settings, "farewell", "s", &str);
733 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "atomic bye-bye")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("atomic bye-bye"); if
(g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 733, ((const char*)
(__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"atomic bye-bye\"", __s1, "=="
, __s2); } while (0);
734 g_free (str);
735 str = NULL((void*)0);
736
737 g_settings_get (settings2, "greeting", "s", &str);
738 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "greetings from test_atomic")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("greetings from test_atomic"
); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 738, ((const char*)

739 g_free (str);
740 str = NULL((void*)0);
741

743 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "atomic bye-bye")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("atomic bye-bye"); if
(g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 743, ((const char*)

750
751/* On Windows the interaction between the C library locale and libintl
752 * (from GNU gettext) is not like on POSIX, so just skip these tests
753 * for now.
754 *
755 * There are several issues:
756 *
757 * 1) The C library doesn't use LC_MESSAGES, that is implemented only
758 * in libintl (defined in its <libintl.h>).
759 *
760 * 2) The locale names that setlocale() accepts and returns aren't in
761 * the "de_DE" style, but like "German_Germany".
762 *
763 * 3) libintl looks at the Win32 thread locale and not the C library
764 * locale. (And even if libintl would use the C library's locale, as
765 * there are several alternative C library DLLs, libintl might be
766 * linked to a different one than the application code, so they
767 * wouldn't have the same C library locale anyway.)
768 */
769
770/* Test that translations work for schema defaults.
771 *
772 * This test relies on the de.po file in the same directory
773 * to be compiled into ./de/LC_MESSAGES/test.mo
774 */
775static void
776test_l10n (void)
777{
778 GSettings *settings;
779 gchar *str;
780 gchar *locale;
781
782 bindtextdomain ("test", locale_dir);
783 bind_textdomain_codeset ("test", "UTF-8");
784
785 locale = g_strdup (setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, NULL((void*)0)));
786
787 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.localized");
788
789 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", "C", TRUE(!(0)));
790 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, "C");
791 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "error-message");
792 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", locale, TRUE(!(0)));
793 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, locale);
794
795 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "Unnamed")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("Unnamed"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 795, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "str" " " "==" " " "\"Unnamed\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while
(0);
796 g_free (str);
797 str = NULL((void*)0);
798
799 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", "de_DE.UTF-8", TRUE(!(0)));
800 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, "de_DE.UTF-8");
801 /* Only do the test if translation is actually working... */
802 if (g_str_equal (dgettext ("test", "\"Unnamed\"")dcgettext ("test", "\"Unnamed\"", 5), "\"Unbenannt\""))
803 {
804 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "error-message");
805
806 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "Unbenannt")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("Unbenannt"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 806, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "str" " " "==" " " "\"Unbenannt\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while
(0);
807 g_free (str);
808 str = NULL((void*)0);
809 }
810 else
811 g_printerr ("warning: translation is not working... skipping test. ");
812
813 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", locale, TRUE(!(0)));
814 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, locale);
815 g_free (locale);
816 g_object_unref (settings);
817}
818
819/* Test that message context works as expected with translated
820 * schema defaults. Also, verify that non-ASCII UTF-8 content
821 * works.
822 *
823 * This test relies on the de.po file in the same directory
824 * to be compiled into ./de/LC_MESSAGES/test.mo
825 */
826static void
827test_l10n_context (void)
828{
829 GSettings *settings;
830 gchar *str;
831 gchar *locale;
832
833 bindtextdomain ("test", locale_dir);
834 bind_textdomain_codeset ("test", "UTF-8");
835
836 locale = g_strdup (setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, NULL((void*)0)));
837
838 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.localized");
839
840 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", "C", TRUE(!(0)));
841 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, "C");
842 g_settings_get (settings, "backspace", "s", &str);
843 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", locale, TRUE(!(0)));
844 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, locale);
845
846 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "BackSpace")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("BackSpace"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 846, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "str" " " "==" " " "\"BackSpace\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while
(0);
847 g_free (str);
848 str = NULL((void*)0);
849
850 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", "de_DE.UTF-8", TRUE(!(0)));
851 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, "de_DE.UTF-8");
852 /* Only do the test if translation is actually working... */
853 if (g_str_equal (dgettext ("test", "\"Unnamed\"")dcgettext ("test", "\"Unnamed\"", 5), "\"Unbenannt\""))
854 {
855 g_settings_get (settings, "backspace", "s", &str);
856
857 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "Löschen")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("Löschen"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 857, ((const char*) (__func__))
, "str" " " "==" " " "\"Löschen\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while
(0);
858 g_free (str);
859 str = NULL((void*)0);
860 }
861 else
862 g_printerr ("warning: translation is not working... skipping test. ");
863
864 g_setenv ("LC_MESSAGES", locale, TRUE(!(0)));
865 setlocale (LC_MESSAGES5, locale);
866 g_free (locale);
867 g_object_unref (settings);
868}

935static void
936test_object_get_property (GObject *object,
937 guint prop_id,
938 GValue *value,
939 GParamSpec *pspec)
940{
941 TestObject *test_object = (TestObject *)object;
942
943 switch (prop_id)
944 {
945 case PROP_BOOL:
946 g_value_set_boolean (value, test_object->bool_prop);
947 break;
948 case PROP_ANTI_BOOL:
949 g_value_set_boolean (value, test_object->anti_bool_prop);
950 break;
951 case PROP_BYTE:
952 g_value_set_schar (value, test_object->byte_prop);
953 break;
954 case PROP_UINT16:
955 g_value_set_uint (value, test_object->uint16_prop);
956 break;
957 case PROP_INT16:
958 g_value_set_int (value, test_object->int16_prop);
959 break;
960 case PROP_INT:
961 g_value_set_int (value, test_object->int_prop);
962 break;
963 case PROP_UINT:
964 g_value_set_uint (value, test_object->uint_prop);
965 break;
966 case PROP_INT64:
967 g_value_set_int64 (value, test_object->int64_prop);
968 break;
969 case PROP_UINT64:
970 g_value_set_uint64 (value, test_object->uint64_prop);
971 break;
972 case PROP_DOUBLE:
973 g_value_set_double (value, test_object->double_prop);
974 break;
975 case PROP_STRING:
976 g_value_set_string (value, test_object->string_prop);
977 break;
978 case PROP_NO_WRITE:
979 g_value_set_string (value, test_object->no_write_prop);
980 break;
981 case PROP_STRV:
982 g_value_set_boxed (value, test_object->strv_prop);
983 break;
984 case PROP_ENUM:
985 g_value_set_enum (value, test_object->enum_prop);
986 break;
987 case PROP_FLAGS:
988 g_value_set_flags (value, test_object->flags_prop);
989 break;
990 default:
991 G_OBJECT_WARN_INVALID_PROPERTY_ID (object, prop_id, pspec)do { GObject *_glib__object = (GObject*) ((object)); GParamSpec
*_glib__pspec = (GParamSpec*) ((pspec)); guint _glib__property_id
= ((prop_id)); g_warning ("%s:%d: invalid %s id %u for \"%s\" of type '%s' in '%s'"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 991, ("property"), _glib__property_id
, _glib__pspec->name, g_type_name ((((((GTypeClass*) (((GTypeInstance
*) (_glib__pspec))->g_class))->g_type)))), (g_type_name
((((((GTypeClass*) (((GTypeInstance*) (_glib__object))->g_class
))->g_type)))))); } while (0);
992 break;
993 }
994}
995
996static void
997test_object_set_property (GObject *object,
998 guint prop_id,
999 const GValue *value,
1000 GParamSpec *pspec)
1001{
1002 TestObject *test_object = (TestObject *)object;
1003
1004 switch (prop_id)
1005 {
1006 case PROP_BOOL:
1007 test_object->bool_prop = g_value_get_boolean (value);
1008 break;
1009 case PROP_ANTI_BOOL:
1010 test_object->anti_bool_prop = g_value_get_boolean (value);
1011 break;
1012 case PROP_BYTE:
1013 test_object->byte_prop = g_value_get_schar (value);
1014 break;
1015 case PROP_INT16:
1016 test_object->int16_prop = g_value_get_int (value);
1017 break;
1018 case PROP_UINT16:
1019 test_object->uint16_prop = g_value_get_uint (value);
1020 break;
1021 case PROP_INT:
1022 test_object->int_prop = g_value_get_int (value);
1023 break;
1024 case PROP_UINT:
1025 test_object->uint_prop = g_value_get_uint (value);
1026 break;
1027 case PROP_INT64:
1028 test_object->int64_prop = g_value_get_int64 (value);
1029 break;
1030 case PROP_UINT64:
1031 test_object->uint64_prop = g_value_get_uint64 (value);
1032 break;
1033 case PROP_DOUBLE:
1034 test_object->double_prop = g_value_get_double (value);
1035 break;
1036 case PROP_STRING:
1037 g_free (test_object->string_prop);
1038 test_object->string_prop = g_value_dup_string (value);
1039 break;
1040 case PROP_NO_READ:
1041 g_free (test_object->no_read_prop);
1042 test_object->no_read_prop = g_value_dup_string (value);
1043 break;
1044 case PROP_STRV:
1045 g_strfreev (test_object->strv_prop);
1046 test_object->strv_prop = g_value_dup_boxed (value);
1047 break;
1048 case PROP_ENUM:
1049 test_object->enum_prop = g_value_get_enum (value);
1050 break;
1051 case PROP_FLAGS:
1052 test_object->flags_prop = g_value_get_flags (value);
1053 break;
1054 default:
1055 G_OBJECT_WARN_INVALID_PROPERTY_ID (object, prop_id, pspec)do { GObject *_glib__object = (GObject*) ((object)); GParamSpec
*_glib__pspec = (GParamSpec*) ((pspec)); guint _glib__property_id
= ((prop_id)); g_warning ("%s:%d: invalid %s id %u for \"%s\" of type '%s' in '%s'"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1055, ("property"), _glib__property_id
, _glib__pspec->name, g_type_name ((((((GTypeClass*) (((GTypeInstance
*) (_glib__pspec))->g_class))->g_type)))), (g_type_name
((((((GTypeClass*) (((GTypeInstance*) (_glib__object))->g_class
))->g_type)))))); } while (0);
1056 break;
1057 }
1058}

1098 g_once_init_leave (&define_type_id, type_id)(__extension__ ({ typedef char _GStaticAssertCompileTimeAssertion_30
[(sizeof *(&define_type_id) == sizeof (gpointer)) ? 1 : -
1] __attribute__((__unused__)); 0 ? (void) (*(&define_type_id
) = (type_id)) : (void) 0; g_once_init_leave ((&define_type_id
), (gsize) (type_id)); }));
1099 }
1100
1101 return define_type_id;
1102}
1103
1104static void
1105test_object_class_init (TestObjectClass *class)
1106{
1107 GObjectClass *gobject_class = G_OBJECT_CLASS (class)((((GObjectClass*) g_type_check_class_cast ((GTypeClass*) ((class
)), (((GType) ((20) << (2))))))));
1108
1109 gobject_class->get_property = test_object_get_property;
1110 gobject_class->set_property = test_object_set_property;
1111 gobject_class->finalize = test_object_finalize;
1112
1113 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_BOOL,
1114 g_param_spec_boolean ("bool", "", "", FALSE(0), G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1115 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_ANTI_BOOL,
1116 g_param_spec_boolean ("anti-bool", "", "", FALSE(0), G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1117 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_BYTE,
1118 g_param_spec_char ("byte", "", "", G_MININT8((gint8) (-((gint8) 0x7f) - 1)), G_MAXINT8((gint8) 0x7f), 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1119 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_INT16,
1120 g_param_spec_int ("int16", "", "", -G_MAXINT16((gint16) 0x7fff), G_MAXINT16((gint16) 0x7fff), 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1121 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_UINT16,
1122 g_param_spec_uint ("uint16", "", "", 0, G_MAXUINT16((guint16) 0xffff), 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1123 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_INT,
1124 g_param_spec_int ("int", "", "", G_MININT(-2147483647 -1), G_MAXINT2147483647, 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1125 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_UINT,
1126 g_param_spec_uint ("uint", "", "", 0, G_MAXUINT(2147483647 *2U +1U), 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1127 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_INT64,
1128 g_param_spec_int64 ("int64", "", "", G_MININT64((gint64) (-(0x7fffffffffffffffL) - (1L))), G_MAXINT64(0x7fffffffffffffffL), 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1129 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_UINT64,
1130 g_param_spec_uint64 ("uint64", "", "", 0, G_MAXUINT64(0xffffffffffffffffUL), 0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1131 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_DOUBLE,
1132 g_param_spec_double ("double", "", "", -G_MAXDOUBLE1.7976931348623157e+308, G_MAXDOUBLE1.7976931348623157e+308, 0.0, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1133 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_STRING,
1134 g_param_spec_string ("string", "", "", NULL((void*)0), G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1135 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_NO_WRITE,
1136 g_param_spec_string ("no-write", "", "", NULL((void*)0), G_PARAM_READABLE));
1137 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_NO_READ,
1138 g_param_spec_string ("no-read", "", "", NULL((void*)0), G_PARAM_WRITABLE));
1139 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_STRV,
1140 g_param_spec_boxed ("strv", "", "", G_TYPE_STRV(g_strv_get_type ()), G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1141 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_ENUM,
1142 g_param_spec_enum ("enum", "", "", test_enum_get_type (), TEST_ENUM_FOO, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1143 g_object_class_install_property (gobject_class, PROP_FLAGS,
1144 g_param_spec_flags ("flags", "", "", test_flags_get_type (), TEST_FLAGS_NONE, G_PARAM_READWRITE));
1145}

1153/* Test basic binding functionality for simple types.
1154 * Verify that with bidirectional bindings, changes on either side
1155 * are notified on the other end.
1156 */
1157static void
1158test_simple_binding (void)
1159{
1160 TestObject *obj;
1161 GSettings *settings;
1162 gboolean b;
1163 gchar y;

1178 obj = test_object_new ();

), __n2 = ((!(0))); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1182, ((const char*

"==" " " "TRUE", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2

1434static void
1435test_bind_writable (void)
1436{
1437 TestObject *obj;
1438 GSettings *settings;
1439 gboolean b;
1440
1441 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.binding");
1442 obj = test_object_new ();
1443
1444 g_object_set (obj, "bool", FALSE(0), NULL((void*)0));
1445
1446 g_settings_bind_writable (settings, "int", obj, "bool", FALSE(0));
1447
1448 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1449 g_assert_true (b)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (b) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_
; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1449, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "b" "' should be TRUE"
); } while (0);
1450
1451 g_settings_unbind (obj, "bool");
1452
1453 g_settings_bind_writable (settings, "int", obj, "bool", TRUE(!(0)));
1454
1455 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1456 g_assert_false (b)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(b)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_
; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1456, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "b" "' should be FALSE"
); } while (0);
1457
1458 g_object_unref (obj);
1459 g_object_unref (settings);
1460}

1462/* Test one-way bindings.
1463 * Verify that changes on one side show up on the other,
1464 * but not vice versa
1465 */
1466static void
1467test_directional_binding (void)
1468{
1469 TestObject *obj;
1470 GSettings *settings;
1471 gboolean b;
1472 gint i;
1473
1474 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.binding");
1475 obj = test_object_new ();
1476
1477 g_object_set (obj, "bool", FALSE(0), NULL((void*)0));
1478 g_settings_set_boolean (settings, "bool", FALSE(0));
1479
1480 g_settings_bind (settings, "bool", obj, "bool", G_SETTINGS_BIND_GET);
1481
1482 g_settings_set_boolean (settings, "bool", TRUE(!(0)));
1483 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1484 g_assert_cmpint (b, ==, TRUE)do { gint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = ((!(0))); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1484, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "TRUE", (
long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0
);
1485
1486 g_object_set (obj, "bool", FALSE(0), NULL((void*)0));
1487 g_assert_cmpint (g_settings_get_boolean (settings, "bool"), ==, TRUE)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_settings_get_boolean (settings, "bool")
), __n2 = ((!(0))); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1487, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "g_settings_get_boolean (settings, \"bool\")" " "
"==" " " "TRUE", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2
, 'i'); } while (0);
1488
1489 g_object_set (obj, "int", 20, NULL((void*)0));
1490 g_settings_set_int (settings, "int", 20);
1491
1492 g_settings_bind (settings, "int", obj, "int", G_SETTINGS_BIND_SET);
1493
1494 g_object_set (obj, "int", 32, NULL((void*)0));
1495 g_assert_cmpint (g_settings_get_int (settings, "int"), ==, 32)do { gint64 __n1 = (g_settings_get_int (settings, "int")), __n2
= (32); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum (
"GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1495, ((const char*) (
__func__)), "g_settings_get_int (settings, \"int\")" " " "=="
" " "32", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i')
; } while (0);
1496
1497 g_settings_set_int (settings, "int", 20);
1498 g_object_get (obj, "int", &i, NULL((void*)0));
1499 g_assert_cmpint (i, ==, 32)do { gint64 __n1 = (i), __n2 = (32); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1499, ((const char*) (__func__)), "i" " " "==" " " "32", (long
double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
1500
1501 g_object_unref (obj);
1502 g_object_unref (settings);
1503}

1505/* Test that type mismatch is caught when creating a binding */
1506static void
1507test_typesafe_binding (void)
1508{
1509 if (!g_test_undefined ()(g_test_config_vars->test_undefined))
1510 return;
1511
1512 if (g_test_subprocess ())
1513 {
1514 TestObject *obj;
1515 GSettings *settings;
1516
1517 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.binding");
1518 obj = test_object_new ();
1519
1520 g_settings_bind (settings, "string", obj, "int", G_SETTINGS_BIND_DEFAULT);
1521
1522 g_object_unref (obj);
1523 g_object_unref (settings);
1524 return;
1525 }
1526 g_test_trap_subprocess (NULL((void*)0), 0, 0);
1527 g_test_trap_assert_failed ()g_test_trap_assertions ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1527, ((const char*) (__func__)), 1, 0);
1528 g_test_trap_assert_stderr ("*not compatible*")g_test_trap_assertions ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1528, ((const char*) (__func__)), 4, "*not compatible*");
1529}
1530
1531static gboolean
1532string_to_bool (GValue *value,
1533 GVariant *variant,
1534 gpointer user_data)
1535{
1536 const gchar *s;
1537
1538 s = g_variant_get_string (variant, NULL((void*)0));
1539 g_value_set_boolean (value, g_strcmp0 (s, "true") == 0);
1540
1541 return TRUE(!(0));
1542}
1543
1544static GVariant *
1545bool_to_string (const GValue *value,
1546 const GVariantType *expected_type,
1547 gpointer user_data)
1548{
1549 if (g_value_get_boolean (value))
1550 return g_variant_new_string ("true");
1551 else
1552 return g_variant_new_string ("false");
1553}
1554
1555static GVariant *
1556bool_to_bool (const GValue *value,
1557 const GVariantType *expected_type,
1558 gpointer user_data)
1559{
1560 return g_variant_new_boolean (g_value_get_boolean (value));
1561}

1563/* Test custom bindings.
1564 * Translate strings to booleans and back
1565 */
1566static void
1567test_custom_binding (void)
1568{
1569 TestObject *obj;
1570 GSettings *settings;
1571 gchar *s;
1572 gboolean b;
1573
1574 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.binding");
1575 obj = test_object_new ();

1578
1579 g_settings_bind_with_mapping (settings, "string",
1580 obj, "bool",
1581 G_SETTINGS_BIND_DEFAULT,
1582 string_to_bool,
1583 bool_to_string,
1584 NULL((void*)0), NULL((void*)0));
1585
1586 g_settings_set_string (settings, "string", "false");
1587 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1588 g_assert_cmpint (b, ==, FALSE)do { gint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = ((0)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1588, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "FALSE",
(long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (
0);
1589
1590 g_settings_set_string (settings, "string", "not true");
1591 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1592 g_assert_cmpint (b, ==, FALSE)do { gint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = ((0)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1592, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "FALSE",
(long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (
0);
1593
1594 g_object_set (obj, "bool", TRUE(!(0)), NULL((void*)0));
1595 s = g_settings_get_string (settings, "string");
1596 g_assert_cmpstr (s, ==, "true")do { const char *__s1 = (s), *__s2 = ("true"); if (g_strcmp0 (
__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1596, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "s" " " "==" " " "\"true\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0
);
1597 g_free (s);
1598
1599 g_settings_bind_with_mapping (settings, "string",
1600 obj, "bool",
1601 G_SETTINGS_BIND_DEFAULT,
1602 string_to_bool, bool_to_bool,
1603 NULL((void*)0), NULL((void*)0));
1604 g_test_expect_message (G_LOG_DOMAIN"GLib-GIO", G_LOG_LEVEL_CRITICAL,
1605 "*binding mapping function for key 'string' returned"
1606 " GVariant of type 'b' when type 's' was requested*");

, 1608, ((const char*) (__func__)));

1612}
1613
1614/* Test that with G_SETTINGS_BIND_NO_CHANGES, the
1615 * initial settings value is transported to the object
1616 * side, but later settings changes do not affect the
1617 * object
1618 */
1619static void
1620test_no_change_binding (void)
1621{
1622 TestObject *obj;
1623 GSettings *settings;
1624 gboolean b;
1625
1626 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.binding");
1627 obj = test_object_new ();
1628
1629 g_object_set (obj, "bool", TRUE(!(0)), NULL((void*)0));
1630 g_settings_set_boolean (settings, "bool", FALSE(0));
1631
1632 g_settings_bind (settings, "bool", obj, "bool", G_SETTINGS_BIND_GET_NO_CHANGES);
1633
1634 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1635 g_assert_cmpint (b, ==, FALSE)do { gint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = ((0)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1635, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "FALSE",
(long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (
0);
1636
1637 g_settings_set_boolean (settings, "bool", TRUE(!(0)));
1638 g_object_get (obj, "bool", &b, NULL((void*)0));
1639 g_assert_cmpint (b, ==, FALSE)do { gint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = ((0)); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1639, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "FALSE",
(long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (
0);
1640
1641 g_settings_set_boolean (settings, "bool", FALSE(0));
1642 g_object_set (obj, "bool", TRUE(!(0)), NULL((void*)0));
1643 b = g_settings_get_boolean (settings, "bool");
1644 g_assert_cmpint (b, ==, TRUE)do { gint64 __n1 = (b), __n2 = ((!(0))); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1644, ((const char*) (__func__)), "b" " " "==" " " "TRUE", (
long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0
);
1645
1646 g_object_unref (obj);
1647 g_object_unref (settings);
1648}

1736static void
1737key_changed_cb (GSettings *settings, const gchar *key, gpointer data)
1738{
1739 gboolean *b = data;
1740 (*b) = TRUE(!(0));
1741}

1744{

1751/*
1752 * Test that using a keyfile works
1753 */
1754static void
1755test_keyfile (Fixture *fixture,
1756 gconstpointer user_data)
1757{
1758 GSettingsBackend *kf_backend;
1759 GSettings *settings;
1760 GKeyFile *keyfile;
1761 gchar *str;
1762 gboolean writable;
1763 GError *error = NULL((void*)0);
1764 gchar *data;
1765 gsize len;
1766 gboolean called = FALSE(0);
1767 gchar *keyfile_path = NULL((void*)0), *store_path = NULL((void*)0);
1768
1769 keyfile_path = g_build_filename (fixture->tmp_dir, "keyfile", NULL((void*)0));
1770 store_path = g_build_filename (keyfile_path, "gsettings.store", NULL((void*)0));
1771 kf_backend = g_keyfile_settings_backend_new (store_path, "/", "root");
1772 settings = g_settings_new_with_backend ("org.ctk.test", kf_backend);
1773 g_object_unref (kf_backend);
1774
1775 g_settings_reset (settings, "greeting");
1776 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "greeting");
1777 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "Hello, earthlings")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("Hello, earthlings");
if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1777, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"Hello, earthlings\"", __s1
, "==", __s2); } while (0);

; if (writable) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0
; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1781, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "'" "writable" "' should be TRUE"); } while (0);
1782 g_settings_set (settings, "greeting", "s", "see if this works");
1783
1784 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "greeting");
1785 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "see if this works")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("see if this works");

("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1785, ((const char*

1790 g_settings_apply (settings);

; if (g_key_file_load_from_file (keyfile, store_path, 0, ((void
*)0))) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_
; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1793, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_key_file_load_from_file (keyfile, store_path, 0, NULL)"
"' should be TRUE"); } while (0);
1794
1795 str = g_key_file_get_string (keyfile, "tests", "greeting", NULL((void*)0));
1796 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "'see if this works'")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("'see if this works'"
); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1796, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"'see if this works'\"", __s1
, "==", __s2); } while (0);
1797 g_free (str);
1798
1799 str = g_key_file_get_string (keyfile, "tests", "farewell", NULL((void*)0));
1800 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "'cheerio'")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("'cheerio'"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1800, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "str" " " "==" " " "\"'cheerio'\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while
(0);
1801 g_free (str);
1802 g_key_file_free (keyfile);
1803
1804 g_settings_reset (settings, "greeting");
1805 g_settings_apply (settings);
1806 keyfile = g_key_file_new ();
1807 g_assert_true (g_key_file_load_from_file (keyfile, store_path, 0, NULL))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (g_key_file_load_from_file (keyfile, store_path, 0, ((void
*)0))) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_
; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1807, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_key_file_load_from_file (keyfile, store_path, 0, NULL)"
"' should be TRUE"); } while (0);
1808

1810 g_assert_null (str)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if ((str) == ((void*)0)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_
= 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1810, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "'" "str" "' should be NULL"); } while (0);

GCallback) (key_changed_cb))), (&called), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags
) 0);
1814

1816 data = g_key_file_to_data (keyfile, &len, NULL((void*)0));
1817 g_file_set_contents (store_path, data, len, &error);
1818 g_assert_no_error (error)do { if (error) g_assertion_message_error ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1818, ((const char*) (__func__)), "error", error, 0, 0); } while
(0);
1819 while (!called)
1820 g_main_context_iteration (NULL((void*)0), FALSE(0));
1821 g_signal_handlers_disconnect_by_func (settings, key_changed_cb, &called)g_signal_handlers_disconnect_matched ((settings), (GSignalMatchType
) (G_SIGNAL_MATCH_FUNC | G_SIGNAL_MATCH_DATA), 0, 0, ((void*)
0), (key_changed_cb), (&called));
1822
1823 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "greeting");
1824 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "howdy")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("howdy"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"

), "str" " " "==" " " "\"howdy\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while
(0);
1825 g_free (str);
1826
1827 /* Now check setting a string without quotes */
1828 called = FALSE(0);
1829 g_signal_connect (settings, "changed::greeting", G_CALLBACK (key_changed_cb), &called)g_signal_connect_data ((settings), ("changed::greeting"), (((
GCallback) (key_changed_cb))), (&called), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags
) 0);
1830

1832 g_free (data);
1833 data = g_key_file_to_data (keyfile, &len, NULL((void*)0));
1834 g_file_set_contents (store_path, data, len, &error);
1835 g_assert_no_error (error)do { if (error) g_assertion_message_error ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1835, ((const char*) (__func__)), "error", error, 0, 0); } while
(0);
1836 while (!called)
1837 g_main_context_iteration (NULL((void*)0), FALSE(0));
1838 g_signal_handlers_disconnect_by_func (settings, key_changed_cb, &called)g_signal_handlers_disconnect_matched ((settings), (GSignalMatchType
) (G_SIGNAL_MATCH_FUNC | G_SIGNAL_MATCH_DATA), 0, 0, ((void*)
0), (key_changed_cb), (&called));
1839
1840 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "greeting");
1841 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "he\"l🤗uń")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("he\"l🤗uń"); if (
g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1841, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"he\\\"l🤗uń\"", __s1,
"==", __s2); } while (0);
1842 g_free (str);
1843
1844 g_settings_set (settings, "farewell", "s", "cheerio");
1845
1846 /* Check that empty keys/groups are not allowed. */
1847 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, ""))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, ""))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1847, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, \"\")"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1848 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, "/"))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, "/"))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1848, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, \"/\")"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1849
1850 /* When executing as root, changing the mode of the keyfile will have
1851 * no effect on the writability of the settings.
1852 */
1853 if (geteuid () != 0)
1854 {
1855 called = FALSE(0);
1856 g_signal_connect (settings, "writable-changed::greeting",g_signal_connect_data ((settings), ("writable-changed::greeting"
), (((GCallback) (key_changed_cb))), (&called), ((void*)0
), (GConnectFlags) 0)
1857 G_CALLBACK (key_changed_cb), &called)g_signal_connect_data ((settings), ("writable-changed::greeting"
), (((GCallback) (key_changed_cb))), (&called), ((void*)0
), (GConnectFlags) 0);

1860 while (!called)
1861 g_main_context_iteration (NULL((void*)0), FALSE(0));
1862 g_signal_handlers_disconnect_by_func (settings, key_changed_cb, &called)g_signal_handlers_disconnect_matched ((settings), (GSignalMatchType
) (G_SIGNAL_MATCH_FUNC | G_SIGNAL_MATCH_DATA), 0, 0, ((void*)
0), (key_changed_cb), (&called));
1863
1864 writable = g_settings_is_writable (settings, "greeting");
1865 g_assert_false (writable)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(writable)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_ =
0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 1865, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "'" "writable" "' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1866 }
1867
1868 g_key_file_free (keyfile);
1869 g_free (data);

1871 g_object_unref (settings);

1875 g_assert_cmpint (g_remove (store_path), ==, 0)do { gint64 __n1 = (remove (store_path)), __n2 = (0); if (__n1
== __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"

"==" " " "0", (long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'

1931
1932 /* Check that empty keys/groups are not allowed. */
1933 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, ""))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, ""))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1933, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, \"\")"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1934 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, "/"))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, "/"))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1934, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, \"/\")"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1935
1936 /* Keys which ghost the root group name are not allowed. This can only be
1937 * tested when the path is `/` as otherwise it acts as a prefix and prevents
1938 * any ghosting. */
1939 if (g_str_equal (test_data->path, "/"))
1940 {
1941 key = g_strdup_printf ("%s/%s", test_data->root_group, "");
1942 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, key))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, key))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1942, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, key)"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1943 g_free (key);
1944
1945 key = g_strdup_printf ("%s/%s", test_data->root_group, "/");
1946 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, key))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, key))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1946, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, key)"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1947 g_free (key);
1948
1949 key = g_strdup_printf ("%s/%s", test_data->root_group, "test-boolean");
1950 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, key))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, key))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1950, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, key)"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1951 g_free (key);
1952 }
1953
1954 g_key_file_free (keyfile);
1955 g_object_unref (settings);
1956
1957 /* Clean up the temporary directory. */
1958 g_assert_no_errno (g_chmod (keyfile_path, 0777))do { int __ret, __errsv; (*__errno_location ()) = 0; __ret = chmod
(keyfile_path, 0777); __errsv = (*__errno_location ()); if (
__ret < 0) { gchar *__msg; __msg = g_strdup_printf ("assertion failed ("
"g_chmod (keyfile_path, 0777)" " >= 0): errno %i: %s", __errsv
, g_strerror (__errsv)); g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1958, ((const char*) (__func__)), __msg); g_free (__msg); }
} while (0);
1959 g_assert_no_errno (g_remove (store_path))do { int __ret, __errsv; (*__errno_location ()) = 0; __ret = remove
(store_path); __errsv = (*__errno_location ()); if (__ret <
0) { gchar *__msg; __msg = g_strdup_printf ("assertion failed ("
"g_remove (store_path)" " >= 0): errno %i: %s", __errsv, g_strerror
(__errsv)); g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1959, ((const char*) (__func__)), __msg); g_free (__msg); }
} while (0);
1960 g_assert_no_errno (g_rmdir (keyfile_path))do { int __ret, __errsv; (*__errno_location ()) = 0; __ret = g_rmdir
(keyfile_path); __errsv = (*__errno_location ()); if (__ret <
0) { gchar *__msg; __msg = g_strdup_printf ("assertion failed ("
"g_rmdir (keyfile_path)" " >= 0): errno %i: %s", __errsv,
g_strerror (__errsv)); g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1960, ((const char*) (__func__)), __msg); g_free (__msg); }
} while (0);
1961 g_free (store_path);
1962 g_free (keyfile_path);
1963}

1965/*
1966 * Test that a keyfile rejects writes to keys outside its root path.
1967 */
1968static void
1969test_keyfile_outside_root_path (Fixture *fixture,
1970 gconstpointer user_data)
1971{
1972 GSettingsBackend *kf_backend;
1973 GSettings *settings;
1974 gchar *keyfile_path = NULL((void*)0), *store_path = NULL((void*)0);
1975
1976 keyfile_path = g_build_filename (fixture->tmp_dir, "keyfile", NULL((void*)0));
1977 store_path = g_build_filename (keyfile_path, "gsettings.store", NULL((void*)0));
1978 kf_backend = g_keyfile_settings_backend_new (store_path, "/tests/basic-types/", "root");
1979 settings = g_settings_new_with_backend_and_path ("org.ctk.test.no-path", kf_backend, "/tests/");
1980 g_object_unref (kf_backend);
1981
1982 g_assert_false (g_settings_is_writable (settings, "test-boolean"))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, "test-boolean"))) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
1982, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "g_settings_is_writable (settings, \"test-boolean\")"
"' should be FALSE"); } while (0);
1983
1984 g_object_unref (settings);
1985
1986 /* Clean up the temporary directory. The keyfile probably doesn’t exist, so
1987 * don’t error on failure. */
1988 g_removeremove (store_path);
1989 g_assert_no_errno (g_rmdir (keyfile_path))do { int __ret, __errsv; (*__errno_location ()) = 0; __ret = g_rmdir
(keyfile_path); __errsv = (*__errno_location ()); if (__ret <
0) { gchar *__msg; __msg = g_strdup_printf ("assertion failed ("
"g_rmdir (keyfile_path)" " >= 0): errno %i: %s", __errsv,
g_strerror (__errsv)); g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 1989, ((const char*) (__func__)), __msg); g_free (__msg); }
} while (0);
1990 g_free (store_path);
1991 g_free (keyfile_path);
1992}

2009 g_object_unref (kf_backend);
2010

; if (!(g_settings_is_writable (settings, "test-boolean"))) _g_boolean_var_

; if (g_settings_is_writable (settings, "child/test-boolean")

; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"

2015

(keyfile_path); __errsv = (*__errno_location ()); if (__ret <

2020 g_free (store_path);

2024/* Test that getting child schemas works
2025 */
2026static void
2027test_child_schema (void)
2028{
2029 GSettings *settings;
2030 GSettings *child;
2031 guint8 byte;
2032
2033 /* first establish some known conditions */
2034 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.basic-types");
2035 g_settings_set (settings, "test-byte", "y", 36);
2036
2037 g_settings_get (settings, "test-byte", "y", &byte);
2038 g_assert_cmpint (byte, ==, 36)do { gint64 __n1 = (byte), __n2 = (36); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2038, ((const char*) (__func__)), "byte" " " "==" " " "36",
(long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (
0);
2039
2040 g_object_unref (settings);
2041
2042 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test");
2043 child = g_settings_get_child (settings, "basic-types");
2044 g_assert_nonnull (child)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if ((child) != ((void*)0)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_
= 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2044, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "'" "child" "' should not be NULL"); } while (0);
2045
2046 g_settings_get (child, "test-byte", "y", &byte);
2047 g_assert_cmpint (byte, ==, 36)do { gint64 __n1 = (byte), __n2 = (36); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2047, ((const char*) (__func__)), "byte" " " "==" " " "36",
(long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (
0);
2048
2049 g_object_unref (child);
2050 g_object_unref (settings);
2051}
2052
2053#include "../strinfo.c"
2054
2055static void
2056test_strinfo (void)
2057{
2058 /* "foo" has a value of 1
2059 * "bar" has a value of 2
2060 * "baz" is an alias for "bar"
2061 */
2062 gchar array[] =
2063 "\1\0\0\0" "\xff""foo" "\0\0\0\xff" "\2\0\0\0"
2064 "\xff" "bar" "\0\0\0\xff" "\3\0\0\0" "\xfe""baz"
2065 "\0\0\0\xff";
2066 const guint32 *strinfo = (guint32 *) array;
2067 guint length = sizeof array / 4;
2068 guint result = 0;
2069
2070 {
2071 /* build it and compare */
2072 GString *builder;
2073
2074 builder = g_string_new (NULL((void*)0));
2075 strinfo_builder_append_item (builder, "foo", 1);
2076 strinfo_builder_append_item (builder, "bar", 2);
2077 g_assert_true (strinfo_builder_append_alias (builder, "baz", "bar"))do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if (strinfo_builder_append_alias (builder, "baz", "bar")) _g_boolean_var_
= 1; else _g_boolean_var_ = 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else
g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c",
2077, ((const char*) (__func__)), "'" "strinfo_builder_append_alias (builder, \"baz\", \"bar\")"
"' should be TRUE"); } while (0);
2078 g_assert_cmpmem (builder->str, builder->len, strinfo, length * 4)do { gconstpointer __m1 = builder->str, __m2 = strinfo; int
__l1 = builder->len, __l2 = length * 4; if (__l1 != 0 &&
__m1 == ((void*)0)) g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2078, ((const char*) (__func__)), "assertion failed (" "builder->len"
" == 0 || " "builder->str" " != NULL)"); else if (__l2 !=
0 && __m2 == ((void*)0)) g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2078, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "assertion failed (" "length * 4" " == 0 || " "strinfo" " != NULL)"
); else if (__l1 != __l2) g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2078, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "builder->len" " (len(" "builder->str" ")) == " "length * 4"
" (len(" "strinfo" "))", (long double) __l1, "==", (long double
) __l2, 'i'); else if (__l1 != 0 && __m2 != ((void*)0
) && memcmp (__m1, __m2, __l1) != 0) g_assertion_message
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2078, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "assertion failed (" "builder->str" " == " "strinfo"
")"); } while (0);
2079 g_string_free (builder, TRUE(!(0)));
2080 }
2081
2082 g_assert_cmpstr (strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length, "foo"),do { const char *__s1 = (strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length
, "foo")), *__s2 = (((void*)0)); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) ==
0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2083, ((const char*) (__func__)), "strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length, \"foo\")"
" " "==" " " "NULL", __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0)
2083 ==, NULL)do { const char *__s1 = (strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length
, "foo")), *__s2 = (((void*)0)); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) ==
0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2083, ((const char*) (__func__)), "strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length, \"foo\")"
" " "==" " " "NULL", __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0);
2084 g_assert_cmpstr (strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length, "bar"),do { const char *__s1 = (strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length
, "bar")), *__s2 = (((void*)0)); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) ==
0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2085, ((const char*) (__func__)), "strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length, \"bar\")"
" " "==" " " "NULL", __s1, "==", __s2); } while (0)
2085 ==, NULL)do { const char *__s1 = (strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length
, "bar")), *__s2 = (((void*)0)); if (g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) ==
0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2085, ((const char*) (__func__)), "strinfo_string_from_alias (strinfo, length, \"bar\")"

2382
2383static gboolean
2384strv_has_string (gchar **haystack,
2385 const gchar *needle)
2386{
2387 guint n;
2388
2389 for (n = 0; haystack != NULL((void*)0) && haystack[n] != NULL((void*)0); n++)
2390 {
2391 if (g_strcmp0 (haystack[n], needle) == 0)
2392 return TRUE(!(0));
2393 }
2394 return FALSE(0);
2395}
2396
2397static gboolean
2398strv_set_equal (gchar **strv, ...)
2399{
2400 gint count;
2401 va_list list;
2402 const gchar *str;
2403 gboolean res;
2404
2405 res = TRUE(!(0));
2406 count = 0;
2407 va_start (list, strv)__builtin_va_start(list, strv);
2408 while (1)
2409 {
2410 str = va_arg (list, const gchar *)__builtin_va_arg(list, const gchar *);
2411 if (str == NULL((void*)0))
2412 break;
2413 if (!strv_has_string (strv, str))
2414 {
2415 res = FALSE(0);
2416 break;
2417 }
2418 count++;
2419 }
2420 va_end (list)__builtin_va_end(list);
2421
2422 if (res)
2423 res = g_strv_length ((gchar**)strv) == count;
2424
2425 return res;
2426}

2483
2484static gboolean
2485map_func (GVariant *value,
2486 gpointer *result,
2487 gpointer user_data)
2488{
2489 gint *state = user_data;
2490 gint v;
2491
2492 if (value)
2493 v = g_variant_get_int32 (value);
2494 else
2495 v = -1;
2496
2497 if (*state == 0)
2498 {
2499 g_assert_cmpint (v, ==, 1)do { gint64 __n1 = (v), __n2 = (1); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2499, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "v" " " "==" " " "1", (long double) __n1, "=="
, (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
2500 (*state)++;
2501 return FALSE(0);
2502 }
2503 else if (*state == 1)
2504 {
2505 g_assert_cmpint (v, ==, 0)do { gint64 __n1 = (v), __n2 = (0); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpnum
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2505, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "v" " " "==" " " "0", (long double) __n1, "=="
, (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0);
2506 (*state)++;
2507 return FALSE(0);
2508 }
2509 else
2510 {
2511 g_assert_null (value)do { if (__builtin_expect (__extension__ ({ int _g_boolean_var_
; if ((value) == ((void*)0)) _g_boolean_var_ = 1; else _g_boolean_var_
= 0; _g_boolean_var_; }), 1)) ; else g_assertion_message ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2511, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "'" "value" "' should be NULL"); } while (0);
2512 *result = g_variant_new_int32 (5);
2513 return TRUE(!(0));
2514 }
2515}

2517static void
2518test_get_mapped (void)
2519{
2520 GSettings *settings;
2521 gint state;
2522 gpointer p;
2523 gint val;
2524
2525 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.mapped");
2526 g_settings_set_int (settings, "val", 1);
2527

2530 val = g_variant_get_int32 ((GVariant*)p);
2531 g_assert_cmpint (val, ==, 5)do { gint64 __n1 = (val), __n2 = (5); if (__n1 == __n2) ; else
g_assertion_message_cmpnum ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"
, 2531, ((const char*) (__func__)), "val" " " "==" " " "5", (
long double) __n1, "==", (long double) __n2, 'i'); } while (0
);
2532
2533 g_variant_unref (p);
2534 g_object_unref (settings);
2535}

2681static void
2682test_actions (void)
2683{
2684 GAction *string, *toggle;
2685 gboolean c1, c2, c3;
2686 GSettings *settings;
2687 gchar *name;
2688 GVariantType *param_type;
2689 gboolean enabled;
2690 GVariantType *state_type;
2691 GVariant *state;
2692
2693 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.basic-types");
2694 string = g_settings_create_action (settings, "test-string");
2695 toggle = g_settings_create_action (settings, "test-boolean");
2696 g_object_unref (settings); /* should be held by the actions */
2697
2698 g_signal_connect (settings, "changed", G_CALLBACK (changed_cb2), &c1)g_signal_connect_data ((settings), ("changed"), (((GCallback)
(changed_cb2))), (&c1), ((void*)0), (GConnectFlags) 0);

2898/* Test that per-desktop values from org.ctk.test.gschema.override

2902static void
2903test_per_desktop (void)

2912

2916 g_test_trap_assert_passed ()g_test_trap_assertions ("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c"

2917 }
2918

2920 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "GNOME")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("GNOME"); if (g_strcmp0
(__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr ("GLib-GIO"
, "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2920, ((const char*) (__func__)
), "str" " " "==" " " "\"GNOME\"", __s1, "==", __s2); } while

2924

(0);

2941/* Test that per-desktop values from org.ctk.test.gschema.override
2942 * are successfully loaded based on the value of $XDG_CURRENT_DESKTOP.
2943 */
2944static void
2945test_per_desktop_subprocess (void)
2946{
2947 GSettings *settings;
2948 TestObject *obj;
2949 gpointer p;
2950 gchar *str;
2951
2952 g_setenv ("XDG_CURRENT_DESKTOP", "GNOME-Classic:GNOME", TRUE(!(0)));
2953
2954 settings = g_settings_new ("org.ctk.test.per-desktop");
2955 obj = test_object_new ();
2956
2957 str = g_settings_get_string (settings, "desktop");
2958 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "GNOME Classic")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("GNOME Classic"); if (
g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2958, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"GNOME Classic\"", __s1, "=="
, __s2); } while (0);
2959 g_free (str);
2960
2961 p = g_settings_get_mapped (settings, "desktop", string_map_func, NULL((void*)0));
2962
2963 str = g_variant_dup_string (p, NULL((void*)0));
2964 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "GNOME Classic")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("GNOME Classic"); if (
g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2964, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"GNOME Classic\"", __s1, "=="
, __s2); } while (0);
2965 g_free (str);
2966
2967 g_variant_unref (p);
2968
2969 g_settings_bind (settings, "desktop", obj, "string", G_SETTINGS_BIND_DEFAULT);
2970
2971 g_object_get (obj, "string", &str, NULL((void*)0));
2972 g_assert_cmpstr (str, ==, "GNOME Classic")do { const char *__s1 = (str), *__s2 = ("GNOME Classic"); if (
g_strcmp0 (__s1, __s2) == 0) ; else g_assertion_message_cmpstr
("GLib-GIO", "../gio/tests/gsettings.c", 2972, ((const char*
) (__func__)), "str" " " "==" " " "\"GNOME Classic\"", __s1, "=="
, __s2); } while (0);
